<div id="review_926367940" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/926367940" />
    <a title="Eliza" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15220898-eliza"><img alt="Eliza" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588523539p2/15220898.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/926367940?book_show_action=true">May 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eliza" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eliza" href="/user/show/15220898-eliza">Eliza</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15220898-eliza?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15220898-eliza?shelf=but-daddy-i-love-him">but-daddy-i-love-him</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15220898-eliza?shelf=mafia">mafia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15220898-eliza?shelf=the-good-kind-of-bad">the-good-kind-of-bad</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer926367940" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8396679855260396700"><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431890566i/14878986.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/><b>Title:</b> Torture to Her Soul<br/><b>Series:</b> Monster in His Eyes #2<br/><b>Author:</b> J.M. Darhower<br/><b>Release Date: </b> 29th September, 2014<br/><b>Rating:</b> 4.25-4.5 "Don't say it unless you mean it" Stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br/> <br/> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396707796i/9175086.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411427910i/11226217._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 5E19582D-FE03-4DF7-AAB5-01656BA37D11_zpsovo9mkaa.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>After reading Monster in his Eyes, I was very excited about what to expect with the rest of the story and how it would develop. In particular I wanted to know how dark Ignazio Vitale could really be and to have a greater understanding of the man. I also recall regarding the first book as more of an introductory </span>
  <span id="freeText8396679855260396700" style="display:none"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431890566i/14878986.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><b>Title:</b> Torture to Her Soul<br><b>Series:</b> Monster in His Eyes #2<br><b>Author:</b> J.M. Darhower<br><b>Release Date: </b> 29th September, 2014<br><b>Rating:</b> 4.25-4.5 "Don't say it unless you mean it" Stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br> <br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396707796i/9175086.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411427910i/11226217._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 5E19582D-FE03-4DF7-AAB5-01656BA37D11_zpsovo9mkaa.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After reading Monster in his Eyes, I was very excited about what to expect with the rest of the story and how it would develop. In particular I wanted to know how dark Ignazio Vitale could really be and to have a greater understanding of the man. I also recall regarding the first book as more of an introductory story. We saw Naz and Karissa "meet" and fall in love. By the end of the book we know that their meeting was not by chance but rather premeditated, on Naz's part and although they subsequently fall in love, this was not part of the original plan but now however; it now plays a vital role in its execution.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411432783i/11227109._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 4C811251-5EFA-4402-9553-4AFC7304755B_zpsph2pxhlk.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>From the prologue alone, I gained a much better understanding of him. I loved being inside his head, it helps that he is a thinker, analytical at that. He likes silence, order and is methodical in most things. He's more ruthless than I gave him credit for in the first book, casual in his manner and thinking of taking a life.<br><br><b>"I heard this saying once, long ago, that I've never forgotten: three may keep a secret, if two of them are dead."</b><br><br>As a result of Naz's earlier actions in the first book, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ killing Karissa's estranged father <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> there are choices that must now be made. Naz's choice to commit to a promise he made to Ray as well as himself, years ago for justice;  which will now be at the price of Karrissa's pain. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411430661i/11226799._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo F21DABFA-B89E-4157-A7BD-C6B3FC7845B0_zpsjhi4fh9n.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Although the story is told from Naz's point of view, Karrissa's choice is to love or hate the man who killed her father, the man who still stalks her mother.<br><br><b> There's something seriously wrong with you. But maybe there's something wrong with me, too, because no matter how much I try to hate you, or how much I want to stay away from you, I can't. I love you, but I don't understand… I don't understand why you'd do it, why you'd do that to me, how you could bring yourself to hurt me when you're supposed to love me, too."</b><br><br>As things become clearer in Naz's mind and there is a moment of clarity from an unlikely source, it does not by any means mean there can be vindication. What started as a crusade for justice has now become a raging battle of inner turmoil and serious threat to what he holds dear, with there own serious consequence.<br><br><b>"I'll die someday, somehow, and I'm not afraid. Death will be a release for me. Until then, I live vicariously through others, watching them reach the point of acceptance, watching as they fight for one more breath.<br>Life never grants them it, not when I'm around."</b><br><br>I enjoyed the speed and movement of the the story, at times still it felt as though we were waiting. Waiting for someone to make the next move, this time however it added to the torture, the ominous undercurrent of knowing every action has a reaction and that, that reaction could impact heavily on Naz and Karissa. He's caught between being the uncaring, unfeeling man he has been for years and being overwhelmed with emotion for Karissa and the fear that either way his decision can cost him, her.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411432783i/11227110._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo C3FAD2F6-8D5F-4C17-8BFC-B79F6711CABF_zpsbrquoikq.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm happy with the way the story concluded, although I won't lie I was on tender hooks down to the last page. I must add, it's also very sexy and has lightness and humour to balance the dark. Naz is not the traditional romantic but he does it so well. <br><br><b> ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review. Thank you!~</b><br><br> <br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br> <br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Twitter" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391768351i/8452934.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a href="http://facebook.com/smokinhotbookblog" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Facebook" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391768485i/8452963.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><a         <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer929549956" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11555816326957011120"><b>5 THIS SERIES IS the BOMB Stars</b><br/><br/><b>I can’t believe it’s over. It’s been awhile since I’ve found a series I absolutely loved from start to finish. I love this author, I love Naz, I love everything about this book!</b><br/><br/>I just can’t contain myself….<br/><br/>Really.. I can’t<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I die, you die<br/><br/>I don’t doubt that for a moment</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Imagine a person that is 100% wrong for you. Imagine a person that can hurt you, make you feel pain, shouldn’t be in your life, but somehow is PERFECT for you? That person would be Naz Does </span>
  <span id="freeText11555816326957011120" style="display:none"><b>5 THIS SERIES IS the BOMB Stars</b><br><br><b>I can’t believe it’s over. It’s been awhile since I’ve found a series I absolutely loved from start to finish. I love this author, I love Naz, I love everything about this book!</b><br><br>I just can’t contain myself….<br><br>Really.. I can’t<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I die, you die<br><br>I don’t doubt that for a moment</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Imagine a person that is 100% wrong for you. Imagine a person that can hurt you, make you feel pain, shouldn’t be in your life, but somehow is PERFECT for you? That person would be Naz Does that make sense? No, but it doesn’t have to.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Love is ugly, and messy. Love makes no sense. And I love him, as impossible as that may be.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I love this love story for the sheer fact it’s simply that. A love story. Karissa and Naz are a ball of issues. He killed her father for heaven sakes. So there’s tension and Karissa is pissed. I loved how Torture to her Soul started. There’s so much angst, so much hate that radiates from Karissa, I’m just gobbling up the pages.<br><br>I also love that it’s completely from Naz’s POV. I love how he sees himself through Karissa’s eyes. Yes, he’s a monster and not because he says so, but because he is. You can see it and it just oozes out of the pages, dripping with blood.<br><br><b>I couldn’t get enough</b><br><br>The second thing I love is Naz’s love for Karissa. It doesn’t make sense and it’s so tortured, yet so beautiful at the same time.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>…she’s the most beautiful when she’s doing nothing. When she thinks nobody’s looking, when she thinks she’s alone.<br><br>I’m with her simply because I want to be. Because I need to be. Because she needs me, I think, and if I’m being honest, I need her just as much.<br><br>What I have with you isn’t blissfully ignorant. It’s real, and it isn’t always pretty but when it’s good, it’s good.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The third thing I love about this book is that I felt everything. I felt the hate, I felt the love, I felt all the emotions. I felt like I was there and I was reliving it through them. This book was PERFECTION and an amazing read.<br><br>These are the books I live for, these are the books I strive to obtain. They are gritty, raw and written so beautifully. If you loved Monster in his Eyes, you will not be disappointed in this one.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21956060.Monster_in_His_Eyes__Monster_in_His_Eyes___1_" title="Monster in His Eyes (Monster in His Eyes, #1) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1398071281s/21956060.jpg" alt="Monster in His Eyes (Monster in His Eyes, #1) by J.M. Darhower" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/917309545" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/1497585368/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=1497585368&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=XGDFEVC3AZJU3ODP" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22021942.Torture_to_Her_Soul__Monster_in_His_Eyes___2_" title="Torture to Her Soul (Monster in His Eyes, #2) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1410779359s/22021942.jpg" alt="Torture to Her Soul (Monster in His Eyes, #2) by J.M. Darhower" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00NP4U422/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00NP4U422&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=LISUY77FMZFBN2GC" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17695374668591720373"><br/><b>TORTURE TO HER SOUL</b> is a continuation of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21956060.Monster_in_His_Eyes__Monster_in_His_Eyes___1_' title='Monster in His Eyes (Monster in His Eyes, #1) by J.M. Darhower' rel='nofollow noopener'>Monster in His Eyes</a> with Naz’s as the narrator. <br/><br/><b>Naz</b> and <b>Karissa's </b> relationship is not in a good place because of certain truths that have been revealed. Karissa is no longer naive to Naz's world. This world was created long before Karissa was born and because of past situations she has become inadvertently part of his world. <br/><br/>Naz is not a good man. He knows that and his family knows that but Karissa wrestles with the idea that inside of him is a decent hu</span>
  <span id="freeText17695374668591720373" style="display:none"><br><b>TORTURE TO HER SOUL</b> is a continuation of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21956060.Monster_in_His_Eyes__Monster_in_His_Eyes___1_" title="Monster in His Eyes (Monster in His Eyes, #1) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">Monster in His Eyes</a> with Naz’s as the narrator. <br><br><b>Naz</b> and <b>Karissa's </b> relationship is not in a good place because of certain truths that have been revealed. Karissa is no longer naive to Naz's world. This world was created long before Karissa was born and because of past situations she has become inadvertently part of his world. <br><br>Naz is not a good man. He knows that and his family knows that but Karissa wrestles with the idea that inside of him is a decent human being. Unfortunately, his past haunts him and leaves him cold and unfeeling except to the one person who has brought light into his world. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411793292i/11276123._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>THREE THINGS TO REMEMBER:</u><br><br>•Regardless of if you were there or not, the day happened. There’s a lesson to be learned there, you know. <b>Life goes on without you</b>. <br><br>•<b>“Never trust someone who only ever smiles at you.”</b> <br>I’m going to remember that next time I meet someone who ONLY ever smiles at me. Kind of creepy when you think about it. Wonder what the person is smiling about that they don't take an interest enough to speak to you. *lol*<br><br>•“It’s a little trick I learned. <b>Whenever a situation makes you nervous, suck on a piece of hard candy. </b> It’s psychological. Your brain thinks if you were in any real danger, you wouldn’t be eating something, so it reasons that you’re perfectly fine.” <br>Yep, I’m totally trying this to see if it works. *fingers crossed* it works. <br><br>For lovers of <i>Monster in His Eyes</i> you'll want to read this dark and twisty resolution to their love story. <br><br>✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦<br><b>Release date: 9/29/2014</b><br>Monster in His Eyes- on sale right now for $.99 (9/26/2014): <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1ngfS0r">http://amzn.to/1ngfS0r</a> <br>Torture to Her Soul: Pre-order | order: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1rrwWQt">http://amzn.to/1rrwWQt</a><br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21956060.Monster_in_His_Eyes__Monster_in_His_Eyes___1_" title="Monster in His Eyes (Monster in His Eyes, #1) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1398071281s/21956060.jpg" alt="Monster in His Eyes (Monster in His Eyes, #1) by J.M. Darhower" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22021942.Torture_to_Her_Soul__Monster_in_His_Eyes___2_" title="Torture to Her Soul (Monster in His Eyes, #2) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1410779359s/22021942.jpg" alt="Torture to Her Soul (Monster in His Eyes, #2) by J.M. Darhower" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>2 part series.<br><br>**Complimentary copy in exchange for an honest review.**<br><br><a href="http://foxyblogs.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

How his mind works. <div id="review_1061667181" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1061667181" />
    <a title="Vanessa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12059859-vanessa"><img alt="Vanessa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576765878p2/12059859.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1061667181?book_show_action=true">Sep 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vanessa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vanessa" href="/user/show/12059859-vanessa">Vanessa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=alpha-assholes-i-love">alpha-assholes-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=my-top-book-boyfriends">my-top-book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=auto-buy-authors">auto-buy-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=dark-and-twisted-reads">dark-and-twisted-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=sexy-billionaires">sexy-billionaires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=super-steamy">super-steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=mind-fucks">mind-fucks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=cried-like-a-little-bitch">cried-like-a-little-bitch</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12059859-vanessa?shelf=6-stars-of-above-and-beyond-awesome">6-stars-of-above-and-beyond-awesome</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1061667181" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer846426630143684494"><b>6 stars!!! <u>Not</u> A Good Guy but a DAMN Good Book!!!!!</b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"It's not the darkness that's terrifying, it's what you might find in it."</b>
</i><br/><br/>Holy hell, what a fantastic book and series! I am speechless! This one is going straight to my All Time Fave Shelf!! Why I waited this long to jump into this series, I will never know! Amazing! OMG, I think I just left a piece of my heart back there in that book. <br/><br/><b>
  <u>My absolute favorite element of this book:</u>
</b><br/><br/>Ignazio Vitale!! Naz has got to be one of the darkest, most f</span>
  <span id="freeText846426630143684494" style="display:none"><b>6 stars!!! <u>Not</u> A Good Guy but a DAMN Good Book!!!!!</b><br><br><i>
  <b>"It's not the darkness that's terrifying, it's what you might find in it."</b>
</i><br><br>Holy hell, what a fantastic book and series! I am speechless! This one is going straight to my All Time Fave Shelf!! Why I waited this long to jump into this series, I will never know! Amazing! OMG, I think I just left a piece of my heart back there in that book. <br><br><b>
  <u>My absolute favorite element of this book:</u>
</b><br><br>Ignazio Vitale!! Naz has got to be one of the darkest, most fucked up, and complex characters I've ever read. I loved him and feared him equally in the first book, but OMG, in this book, he is terrifying! Naz hasn't changed one bit, and isn't going to. He's still the best at what he does, and he does it with precision and without fail. I just wanted to know more and more about him. This really is a story about what happens when the love of your life is a bad guy...a guy who is 100% WRONG for you, who has long since passed any chance of redemption. <br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/TorturetoherSoulTeaser_zps9b7cbe9b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414450933i/11656382._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo TorturetoherSoulTeaser_zps9b7cbe9b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <u>My Second Favorite Element of this book:</u>
</b><br><br>The way Naz loves Karissa. OMG!!! For as much of an evil bastard as Naz is, I just wanted to hug him. I loved how patient he was with her, even when she couldn't stand the sight of him. How he would protect her, lay down his life for her, just do anything to keep her safe. So endearing. And oh once again, the sex between these two is hot, hot, hot!!! Holy HELL the scene in Rome on the balcony?!?!? SCORCHING!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>"…she’s the most beautiful when she’s doing nothing. When she thinks nobody’s looking, when she thinks she’s alone."<br><br>"I’m with her simply because I want to be. Because I need to be. Because she needs me, I think, and if I’m being honest, I need her just as much."<br><br>"Don't worry about it," I say quietly, running my thumb across her lips before leaning down and kissing her. "You have no reason to be afraid. I'm not going to hurt you...nobody is." <br>"How can you be sure?" <br>"Because I won't let them," I say. "It's as simple as that."</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/TorturetoherSoulTeaser2_zps22658b5b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414457991i/11657114._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo TorturetoherSoulTeaser2_zps22658b5b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And for all the Karissa haters..LOL. Kidding.. kinda. I really do think the readers were too hard on her, but, I think you will be happy to know that she is more mature in this book. She's just super conflicted. She loves Naz, but she hates that she does. She's fighting it. She doesn't understand how she can love HIM! <br><br>If you love mafia romances, this series is def for you. I know I will be rereading it at least once. What I look for most in a book is for it to make me feel the characters and their emotions. This book is <i>exclusively </i> in Naz's POV, and wow, did I feel this character. I didn't always like the things that he did, but by being in his head, I understood why he did them. But don't get me wrong, this book has some disturbing shit in it. Not in the sense that a lot of the other "dark" books out there right now do. It's not a Stokholm and there isn't really any BDSM themes...maybe one. But in the sense that some of Naz's decisions are hard to swallow. I would be like, no Naz...you're not really gonna, are you?....oh, yep....he did!! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Like the fact that he killed her mother...OH why Naz?! Why did you have to do it? I get that she sealed her own fate when she shot at him, and that it turned into this whole kill or be killed game between them, but I so badly wanted him to be a good guy here. That is one aspect of the story that I will be pondering for a while to come. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I do seriously applaud Darhower for maintaining the consistency of this character throughout this entire story. That is something that is not executed well enough in a lot of the other dark romances out there, in my opinion. There's a definite ARC and transition, but at the last page of this book, Naz is still the ruthless bad boy that he was at the start of it all. <br><br>I need to read more from this author like very soon!! Perfect ending to the series. Everything came full circle and all of my questions were answered. Some of the scenes at the end, like when he went to visit Maria, had me bawling!!!! Loved the much needed light-hearted moments of humor. Like the scene at the dealership with the passport? OMG, hilarious!<br><br>And gah, LOVED that epilogue and bonus scene!!! ❤️<br><br><b>
  <i>"Maybe you're not a good man-" <br>"I'm not." <br>She stalls at my interruption before finishing her thought. "Okay, but that doesn't mean you're a bad man, Naz."<br><br>“It's okay to admit the darkness terrified me. Because I found some light in it. I found her.”<br><br>“I'm not a good man," he says, "but I'm trying. I'm trying. I can't make you any promises of perfection. I can't promise I'll be what you deserve, or what you need, or even what you always want. All I can promise is that I'll love you until the day I die, and I'll spend every moment I'm alive trying for you.” </i>
</b> &lt;--- My very fave quote of the whole book! ❤️ <br><br><a href="http://s996.photobucket.com/user/Vanessa_RB-Babe/media/Torturetohersoulcollage_zps2e659916.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414459628i/11657311._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Torturetohersoulcollage_zps2e659916.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I know I went a little overboard with the quotes here. I just couldn't help myself! I highlighted most of the damn book! These are all just some of my faves. So really, this is half review/ half tribute! Oh and ladies, Naz is MINE!! So read him, enjoy him, fear him, but then get your little paws off!!! ;)<br><br>Long live Naz!! ❤️ ❤️ ❤️</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="846426630143684494" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2449085191" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12356673626173212760"><b>“It's not the darkness that's terrifying, it's what you might find in it.”</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1531367764ra/25960921.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>My love affair (in my mind) with Ignazio Michele Vitale (Naz) continues in this the next book in the “Monster in Her Eyes series. In this book, the author gives voice to Naz as it is written entirely in his (first person) POV. He bares his soul for us and recounts his monstrous deeds and how he came to be the man he is. Naz confides to the reader abut the darkness he feels within and without. He describes the pervasive qua</span>
  <span id="freeText12356673626173212760" style="display:none"><b>“It's not the darkness that's terrifying, it's what you might find in it.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1531367764ra/25960921.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>My love affair (in my mind) with Ignazio Michele Vitale (Naz) continues in this the next book in the “Monster in Her Eyes series. In this book, the author gives voice to Naz as it is written entirely in his (first person) POV. He bares his soul for us and recounts his monstrous deeds and how he came to be the man he is. Naz confides to the reader abut the darkness he feels within and without. He describes the pervasive quality of this darkness:<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> “It's that heavy sort of darkness, the kind you can feel when you breathe, the denseness filling your lungs and slowly suffocating you.”</b>
</blockquote><br>He also tells us a secret:<br><blockquote>
  <b>“I, Ignazio Vitale, have always been afraid of the dark. If you tell anyone that, I'll kill you.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>In the opening chapters, we find Karissa barely speaking to Naz. She goes about her days in a robotic manner, at times even acting downright disrespectful to Naz. Karissa is angry because she felt Naz lied to her by omission. Naz claims he never uttered an untruth to her and never will. Yes, Karissa is angry; but…the reader can still feel the gravitational pull between Karissa and Naz.<br>Naz reflects on his attraction, attachment and love of Karissa. He feels almost entirely dark, yet his heart still beats, and it beats for Karissa. She is precious light to him. She reminds him of the man he used to be before all the darkness shrouded his life.<br><br>As Naz searches his soul and takes stock of his life through the events in this second book, I find the writing deeply reflective with thoughts well organized and flowing from one idea to the next. It’s not just unnecessary filler. No, this writer has something to say to us through her characters…actually she has many things to say.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1531367764i/25960922._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>As you get further into the read, momentum begins to build, and the pace of the plot accelerates exponentially. There are heart-stopping life and death moments and complications that generate intrigue and a vital decision Naz ultimately needs to make. <br><br>And yes…the heat. Oh, the sensational passionate erotic love scenes!!! So beautifully done. So captivating. So worthy of sighs, swoons and… not a little sweat. Naz wants to please in this book. Help me…“io muoio.”<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1531368065ra/25960931.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Naz moves from his dark, dark world toward something he never thought he ever would again…the light of a pure innocent unafraid love. He is reconsidering whether he is completely bad because he thinks himself so and is there a possibility for him to think of himself in another way…the way Karissa does?<br><blockquote>
  <b>“Despite everything she knows I've done, despite most of the time hating me, she can't let go of that sliver of hope, that part of her that thought she saw some good in me somewhere. I told her she couldn't change me, but she didn't believe that shit for a second. I wish... I fucking wish... some part of me could let her be right about this.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1531367764ra/25960923.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Karissa’s “torture to her soul” is in the epiphany she makes after witnessing the choices Naz made.<br><blockquote>
  <b>"Because you can't go back and change things once they're done. You can't rewrite history. Dwelling on it, wondering what could've been different, wondering how things might be in a perfect world, is a waste of time. Because this world isn't perfect, life isn't perfect, and it never will be…”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>This book, this series, this man, Naz is haunting. If you swoon for that bad, bad devil of a man who cannot help but find himself transformed in part by love despite the improbability, then my friend this book, this series, this man was created for you!!!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“It's okay to admit the darkness terrified me. Because I found some light in it. I found her.”</b>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="12356673626173212760" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer942297984" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1914833347962663034"> <b>4 Dark Side Stars.</b><br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412201130i/11339225._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>	<br/>This time we’re inside Naz’s head immediately after the end of the first book. <br/>He never meant to fall in love with Karissa, but that happened anyway and now he doesn’t want to let her go. She belongs to him. <br/>However, the recent events put a strain on their relationship and now she almost don’t even look at him. He knows he have to fight for her but she also knows that he has a dark side and she fears that hidden side of him. <br/>This is a fight that Naz isn’t willing to lose, be</span>
  <span id="freeText1914833347962663034" style="display:none"> <b>4 Dark Side Stars.</b><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412201130i/11339225._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>	<br>This time we’re inside Naz’s head immediately after the end of the first book. <br>He never meant to fall in love with Karissa, but that happened anyway and now he doesn’t want to let her go. She belongs to him. <br>However, the recent events put a strain on their relationship and now she almost don’t even look at him. He knows he have to fight for her but she also knows that he has a dark side and she fears that hidden side of him. <br>This is a fight that Naz isn’t willing to lose, because we will fight against anything that try to Karissa from him…. Including herself. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402872274i/10002999.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4 Stars. <br> <b>Storyline: </b> A gritty and emotional romance story, that will certainly please lovers of dark-and-twisted-romance books. I will always love JM Darhower because she wrote “Sempre” and although these books haven’t the same effect on me (by far) for someone who isn’t usually a fan of twisted romances, these books definitely made my day! <br> <b>Writing Style: </b> First Person. Male POV. Emotional, gritty and completely addictive. <br> <b>Character Development: </b> Karissa was a little stubborn on the beginning and although it was comprehensible where she came from, it annoyed me a little. I liked how she eventually embraced her love and made up her mind. I loved how Naz didn’t suddenly turn into a saint. Yes, his love for Karissa definitely tamed him a little, but he wasn’t a nice guy. Which was good. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Some hot scenes. <br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1028075224" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1028075224" />
    <a title="Peek At My Book Review" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review"><img alt="Peek At My Book Review" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1414761368p2/18263404.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1028075224?book_show_action=true">Aug 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Peek At My Book Review" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Peek At My Book Review" href="/user/show/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review">Peek At My Book Review</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18263404-peek-at-my-book-review?shelf=2014">2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1028075224" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17957835965954028990"><b>Rating:</b> <b> A WOW 4.5 stars </b><br/><br/><b>Ignazio Vitale</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/416927.gif' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>My Views:</b> The fact that it is narrated by Naz had me hooked. God being in that man’s mind is a unique experience…to know what he thinks and how he feels about himself and his actions. This first one-third part of the story consist of the re-construction of the relationship of Naz and Karissa which lets us know the feelings of Naz towards Karissa. Then there are some actions that take place and a serious WTF moment that involve Carmela… Then the rest consist</span>
  <span id="freeText17957835965954028990" style="display:none"><b>Rating:</b> <b> A WOW 4.5 stars </b><br><br><b>Ignazio Vitale</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/416927.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>My Views:</b> The fact that it is narrated by Naz had me hooked. God being in that man’s mind is a unique experience…to know what he thinks and how he feels about himself and his actions. This first one-third part of the story consist of the re-construction of the relationship of Naz and Karissa which lets us know the feelings of Naz towards Karissa. Then there are some actions that take place and a serious WTF moment that involve Carmela… Then the rest consist of Karissa wanting to know more of Naz and understanding him, his actions and redeeming him (or at least trying to) and Naz continuing with his routine, only now each time caring about what Karissa thinks of him and ends up with even more actions and revelations… <br><br><b>
  <i>…three may keep a secret, if two of them are dead. I've spilled many secrets in my life, secrets that always ended up with somebody dying. Sometimes because of me, and other times... well... because of me. </i>
</b><br><br><b>Style of writing:</b> I am a great fan of Miss Darhower’s writing style and I must say that this is not the first male pov that she has written in her books, and she did a fantastic job with Naz here. I somehow found a little resemblance between Naz here and Corrado Moretti from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17838379.Sempre_Redemption__Forever___2_" title="Sempre Redemption (Forever, #2) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">Sempre: Redemption</a>. Since her first book was from Karissa’s pov I thank her from the bottom of my heart for Naz’s pov here. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412164017ra/11333820.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">. However, I am not fan of only one of the protagonists’ pov, I love when I get double/multiple pov as here I could not get to know what Karissa was doing or thinking which was kind of irritating but <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418118ra/827672.gif" width="75" height="35" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> it was important to maintain suspense. <br><br><b>
  <i>She's not just under my skin, she's in my organs, wrapped up in my cells, infecting me</i>
</b><br><br><b>Characters:</b> 1. Let’s talk about Naz <img src="https://p.gr-assets.com/540x540/fit/hostedimages/1380222758/362766.gif%20" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> first, since it’s in his pov. I really liked being in his head (well literally) and we get more about him which was missing in the first book as Naz was supposed to be this mysterious character but here we get to know more from his past and also his family. I really like the fact that we get to know the man Naz is, not only the dangerous man or the murderer but his soft side, more humane side. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412164017ra/11333821.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i> I do what I want, take what I want, and make no apologies for any of it. After all, I wasn't born this way. The world made me who I am, and the world pays for that mistake every day</i>
</b><br><br><b>Favorite Part:</b> The end of the Bonus Scene <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1398443918ra/9414387.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did not work?</b> There are certain things that were left unrevealed/unmentioned <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1412164017ra/11333822.gif" width="75" height="35" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> in the book for instance Brandy (and her actions), Ray (he was another mystery), and I wanted to know why Carmela went back and didn’t pursue Naz…It left me pondering…and then I think that Karissa forgave Naz a bit too quickly (concerning Carmela) <br><br><b> Similar books?</b> None so far<br><br><b> Recommended:</b> Yes…after reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/21956060.Monster_in_His_Eyes__Monster_in_His_Eyes___1_" title="Monster in His Eyes (Monster in His Eyes, #1) by J.M. Darhower" rel="nofollow noopener">Monster in His Eyes</a><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="17957835965954028990" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1552921868" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1552921868" />
    <a title="FMABookReviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15988565-fmabookreviews"><img alt="FMABookReviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1524337358p2/15988565.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1552921868?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="FMABookReviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="FMABookReviews" href="/user/show/15988565-fmabookreviews">FMABookReviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/23254701-torture-to-her-soul">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15988565-fmabookreviews?shelf=5-it-fed-my-addiction-stars">5-it-fed-my-addiction-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15988565-fmabookreviews?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1552921868" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer770862423181326560">I have <strong>never</strong> moved from one book to another without having finished the first book's review. Does that make sense? I have a bad case of OCD coupled with a poor memory, so if I don't write my review right away, I feel slightly unhinged and clueless.<br/><br/>Well, <em>'Torture to Her Soul'</em> was the exception. Because the moment I finished it, <em>'Target on Our Backs'</em> hit my Kindle. This series is that good, that I didn't want to stop. So bear with me. This will be a short review, (like my memory) but that doesn't </span>
  <span id="freeText770862423181326560" style="display:none">I have <strong>never</strong> moved from one book to another without having finished the first book's review. Does that make sense? I have a bad case of OCD coupled with a poor memory, so if I don't write my review right away, I feel slightly unhinged and clueless.<br><br>Well, <em>'Torture to Her Soul'</em> was the exception. Because the moment I finished it, <em>'Target on Our Backs'</em> hit my Kindle. This series is that good, that I didn't want to stop. So bear with me. This will be a short review, (like my memory) but that doesn't make this book any less outstanding.<br><blockquote>
  ❝I'm the kind of man who easily slips between the dark and the light, the kind of monster who walks along the shadows.❞
</blockquote><br>Told in Naz's POV, <em>'Torture to Her Soul'</em> was haunting, exhilarating, stunning and heartbreaking. Darhower brilliantly captured Naz's voice. Getting inside his head was a dark place to be. Naz is not a good man. Is he an anti-hero? Perhaps. But he certainly isn't the kind of man a parent would want for their daughter. Or is he?<br><blockquote>
  ❝She's not just under my skin, she's in my organs, wrapped up in my cells, infecting me.❞
</blockquote><br>We see Naz's struggle between the monster who wants revenge and the man who wants to love (and be loved). He is torn. He wants to hurt Karissa, yet he doesn't. He wants to love her, yet he knows that will hurt her. So while this book is named 'Torture to Her Soul', I actually felt the torture Naz was feeling. He faces his demons. He accepts who he is and yet wants to be better.<br><br>I love their romance, their story, their love. They both struggle with what's right and what's wrong and try to fit their relationship within those boxes. But is real love like that? Is it always right, or always wrong? Or is it somewhere in between?<br><br>I loved it! If you haven't started this series yet, I highly recommend it!<br><br><a href="http://feedingmyaddictionbookreviews.com" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1440995431i/16050160.jpg" alt="goodreads banner" width="400" height="140" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> </span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14908669408620481921">First, I would like to thank the author for writing this book from Ignazio Vitale's pov. I am sooooooo grateful for it!!<br/><br/>Second, please tell me I'm not the only one head over heels for Naz????!!!! He's amazing! Getting to see everything through his eyes gave me a chance to try to understand what motivated him. To get why he made the choices he did. There were parts of this story that were absolutely gut-wrenching <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ such as when he told what happened the night Johnny came to kill him</span></span>
  <span id="freeText14908669408620481921" style="display:none">First, I would like to thank the author for writing this book from Ignazio Vitale's pov. I am sooooooo grateful for it!!<br /><br />Second, please tell me I'm not the only one head over heels for Naz????!!!! He's amazing! Getting to see everything through his eyes gave me a chance to try to understand what motivated him. To get why he made the choices he did. There were parts of this story that were absolutely gut-wrenching <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ such as when he told what happened the night Johnny came to kill him and his wife <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and parts that made me laugh. I liked seeing that Naz really had a sense of humour despite his cold appearance. His inner thoughts around people was hilarious! Especially with Paul. And I loved how OCD he was with his things, such as his kitchen and his "trunk".<br /><br />I'm not sure how I felt about the <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[visiting Maria's grave <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>scene. I couldn't figure out if it was to underline how much he still loved her or if it was to show that through his grief he was able to find love again. He said he felt guilty for what he had with Karissa and it kind of pissed me off. I completely understood it, don't get me wrong, but it still annoyed me.<br /><br />I'm glad that it didn't take too long for Naz to see Ray's true colours. It's just sad all around. But I am happy that everyone got their just desserts lol.<br /><br />So after some ups and many downs, Naz and Karissa got their HFN. I wonder how long it really lasts considering there is a third book! Can't wait to read that one and I hope it's in Naz's pov again. I cannot get enough of this character!!</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1099431743" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15865466043864735957"><br/><b>4.5 Perfectly Imperfect Stars!</b><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/22C7D568-6AE8-4A67-9265-8F377C14C065_zpsornlf7ca.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415542435i/11808348._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 22C7D568-6AE8-4A67-9265-8F377C14C065_zpsornlf7ca.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Ya know that feeling when you're reading a book, one of hundreds you read per year, and something just stands out. Something about the writing that appears to reach out from the pages, grab ahold of you and not let go? Now, if this was Naz grabbing, he'd probably <i>really</i> not let go, but I digress. It's the kind of writing that plucks you smack dab into their story where you feel personally invested, physically responding to the scenes before you...heart racing, n</span>
  <span id="freeText15865466043864735957" style="display:none"><br><b>4.5 Perfectly Imperfect Stars!</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/22C7D568-6AE8-4A67-9265-8F377C14C065_zpsornlf7ca.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415542435i/11808348._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 22C7D568-6AE8-4A67-9265-8F377C14C065_zpsornlf7ca.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Ya know that feeling when you're reading a book, one of hundreds you read per year, and something just stands out. Something about the writing that appears to reach out from the pages, grab ahold of you and not let go? Now, if this was Naz grabbing, he'd probably <i>really</i> not let go, but I digress. It's the kind of writing that plucks you smack dab into their story where you feel personally invested, physically responding to the scenes before you...heart racing, nether region fluttering...yah, you know. Well, this author did that for me. Not many can do that, especially when it's a darker, twisted read. I've come to expect the unexpected. But I didn't expect this...<br><br><br><b>Tortured to Her Soul</b>, the sequel to Monster in His Eyes, picks up on right where we left off. However, what makes this book "unputdownable" is that it's in Naz' POV. The dangerous enigma of a man finally gets his story. If I didn't love him enough before, I do even more now. He's been through so much, is guilty for so much, yet I found him an endearing, impossible-not-to-love (anti)-hero.<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/CB0E6540-F7E1-4E57-9BFA-2519EEE7B1F6_zps7mrk8mvo.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415543118i/11808481._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo CB0E6540-F7E1-4E57-9BFA-2519EEE7B1F6_zps7mrk8mvo.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>This book I refuse to spoil. Step on the ride. You won't want to jump off. We know Naz isn't a good man. We know his biggest weakness is Karissa yet his biggest drive is revenge. Can he have both? Not likely. So, what's the decision he makes? He's promised never to purposefully hurt Karissa. Is this the first promise he will break? Can he survive the fallout if he does? He knows he should let Karissa go. He's a dark monster within a shell of a man. But she's his light...<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Used%20in%20review/F8EF81BE-BB31-44EF-ADBF-EA9454B63F86_zpsnnovpfpx.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415471045i/11795234._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo F8EF81BE-BB31-44EF-ADBF-EA9454B63F86_zpsnnovpfpx.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I haven't devoured a series like this in a long time. I was in a bit of a slump and this was the perfect mind boggling series to get me out. It's got it all...mystery, intrigue, darkness, heat, and a love story buried beneath it all. I loved it! Recommend to anyone who likes all of the above elements. Looking forward to reading more from Ms Darhower!<br><br><br>And I thank you!<br><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/user/allipalk/media/Blowing%20Kisses/683531EA-D7A1-4AD8-AE04-AACB6D124E2D_zpsafqd4fka.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411671763ra/11263667.gif" alt=" photo 683531EA-D7A1-4AD8-AE04-AACB6D124E2D_zpsafqd4fka.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

    <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga"><img alt="Beatrice Masaluñga" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603719912p2/4590441.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1751212966?book_show_action=true">Sep 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beatrice Masaluñga" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beatrice Masaluñga" href="/user/show/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga">Beatrice Masaluñga</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga?shelf=favorite-books">favorite-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4590441-beatrice-masalu-ga?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1751212966" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7416866694870225131"><i>Torture to Her Soul</i> begins from the end of the previous book and it's told in <b>Ignazio Vitale's</b> point of view. At first, I find it difficult to connect with his story. Maybe because its tone is darker and more melodramatic than Karissa's. As the chapters go on, I slowly immersed on his narration and it somewhat grew on me. <br/><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“People make mistakes. They do things sometimes that you don't like, that you wouldn't do. But that doesn't mean you should give up on them, that you should write them </blockquote></b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText7416866694870225131" style="display:none"><i>Torture to Her Soul</i> begins from the end of the previous book and it's told in <b>Ignazio Vitale's</b> point of view. At first, I find it difficult to connect with his story. Maybe because its tone is darker and more melodramatic than Karissa's. As the chapters go on, I slowly immersed on his narration and it somewhat grew on me. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“People make mistakes. They do things sometimes that you don't like, that you wouldn't do. But that doesn't mean you should give up on them, that you should write them off. Because nobody is hopeless as long as they're still breathing.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br /><br /><br />Revelations, lies and betrayals damaged his relationship with Karissa. What he did was unforgivable and it sparked her hate and anger towards him. He's being patient on moments she pushed his buttons. He understands the hurt she's feeling and gives her the space she needs. Despite of the silent treatment and distance between them, he truly loves her and deep down she's feeling the same way. It's not an easy journey for them to work out their relationship and gained each others trust.<br /><br />His past made him a vulnerable, broken man. He will not forgive himself and the people who caused his love ones death. A part of him died and he will never be the same again. He's going to have revenge and there's a lot to pay. Unexpectedly, Karissa is an innocent, sweet and loving woman he never thought of. Despite of her bloodline, she gave him light to his darkness. He <i>lived</i> being with her and instead of killing her, he fell in love with her and he will do everything to keep her safe.<br /><br /><b>These two have amazing character developments. They handled their personal and relationship issues maturely.</b> I love how Karissa accepts Naz's flaws. His actions made him a bad guy but she believed that there's goodness in him. I love Naz for being honest with his feelings, he doesn't sugarcoat anything and bared it all. <b>The chemistry between them is SIZZLING HOTTER than the first book. JALAPEÑO HOT.</b> Goodness, I freaking love the romance between them. The last chapters are pretty intense and a little emotional. It also put me on the edge of my seat. The epilogue and the bonus scene was hands down amazing! This is truly a promising sequel. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7416866694870225131" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('4E5VOa2Ur0zHEDoi2WzMZe2MNOAF+98VRJEX2YEJ/nUo8aEF7995FriMeWt5kUkSlj0j2Cevp59hvIRFKN/WIA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }
